Error: etcdserver: mvcc: required revision has been compacted. · Issue #58067 · kubernetes/kubernetes\",\"url\":\"https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/58067\"},{\"title\":\"1537270 – logspam: etcdserver: mvcc: required revision has been compacted\",\"url\":\"https://bugzilla.redhat.com/show_bug.cgi?id=1537270\"},{\"title\":\"etcdserver: mvcc: required revision has been compacted in OpenShift etcd log - This MVCC (Multi-Version Concurrency Control) error occurs when a client tries to access or watch at a revision number that no longer exists because etcd has compacted (removed) that historical data.\n\n## When It Occurs\n\nThis typically manifests when: A Kubernetes API watcher tries to reconnect at an old revision, clients request historical key-value states that have been deleted, or cluster members are out of sync, with newer members compacting data faster than older ones can access it. This error commonly occurs in Kubernetes clusters when etcd automatically cleans up historical data to manage storage space.\n\n## Why Compaction Happens\n\nSince etcd keeps an exact history of its keyspace, this history should be periodically compacted to avoid performance degradation and eventual storage space exhaustion. Compacting the keyspace history drops all information about keys superseded prior to a given keyspace revision. This MVCC (Multi-Version Concurrency Control) error occurs when a client tries to access or watch at a revision number that no longer exists because etcd has compacted (removed) that historical data.\n\n## When It Occurs\n\nThis typically manifests when: A Kubernetes API watcher tries to reconnect at an old revision, clients request historical key-value states that have been deleted, or cluster members are out of sync, with newer members compacting data faster than older ones can access it. This error commonly occurs in Kubernetes clusters when etcd automatically cleans up historical data to manage storage space.\n\n## Why Compaction Happens\n\nSince etcd keeps an exact history of its keyspace, this history should be periodically compacted to avoid performance degradation and eventual storage space exhaustion. Compacting the keyspace history drops all information about keys superseded prior to a given keyspace revision. This is a normal operational behavior that prevents etcd from running out of disk space.\n\nThe error appears frequently in real Kubernetes deployments across versions 1.8+, including Kubernetes, K3s, and Rancher clusters."],"durationSeconds":8.527689013}}

The function is located in the `mvcc/kvstore_txn.go` file.\n\n### Key Characteristics:\n\nThe rangeKeys function is called to complete read operations - it takes the key and the relevant revision, queries the treeIndex to find which revisions satisfy the specified conditions, then retrieves the corresponding key-value pairs from boltdb and returns them as a RangeResult.\n\n### Implementation Details:\n\nThe function handles different scenarios, including returning an error when checking for compaction, and when Count is set in RangeOptions, it calls `tr.s.kvindex.CountRevisions` to count revisions matching the key range.\n\n### Context in MVCC Architecture:\n\nRange operations in read transactions read from both a copy of the backend read buffer and the boltdb transaction, allowing the transaction to not block following changes to the backend read buffer.\n\nThe function plays a central role in etcd's multi-version concurrency control system by enabling point-in-time reads at specific revisions while maintaining isolation and consistency.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5284af8e-6b8d-4612-9e2f-71092021ab61","uuid":"e59b06a8-9783-4f53-9999-e634a2e62a26","tool_use_result":{"query":"etcd mvcc rangeKeys function kvstore.go implementation","results":[{"tool_use_id":"srvtoolu_011sAcoF5rHs5gkLahrRwFiG","content":[{"title":"mvcc package - Here are the key findings:\n\n## ErrCompacted Error Definition\n\nThe error is defined in etcd's mvcc package as: `ErrCompacted = errors.New(\"mvcc: required revision has been compacted\")`\n\n## What This Error Means\n\nThe \"etcdserver: mvcc: required revision has been compacted\" error indicates that an etcd client or watcher is attempting to access a revision that has already been removed from the database through the compaction process.\n\nThe MVCC (Multi-Version Concurrency Control) error occurs when a client tries to access or watch at a revision number that no longer exists because etcd has compacted (removed) that historical data. When etcd compacts its database, it permanently removes all information about keys that existed before the compaction revision, making those revisions inaccessible.\n\n## Common Causes\n\nThis typically manifests when a Kubernetes API watcher tries to reconnect at an old revision, clients request historical key-value states that have been deleted, or cluster members are out of sync, with newer members compacting data faster than older ones can access it.\n\n## Why Compaction Happens\n\nSince etcd keeps an exact history of its keyspace, this history should be periodically compacted to avoid performance degradation and eventual storage space exhaustion. Compacting the keyspace history drops all information about keys superseded prior to a given keyspace revision.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5284af8e-6b8d-4612-9e2f-71092021ab61","uuid":"08efbf58-b6fc-4259-84bf-d398a6dff415","tool_use_result":{"query":"etcd mvcc/error.go OR mvcc/errors.go ErrCompacted \"required revision has been compacted\"","results":[{"tool_use_id":"srvtoolu_01WdV1tRuoP8Y6cpC2SR7G2C","content":[{"title":"Kubernetes 1.8.3 -
